    "Spectral data\n",
    "-------------\n",
    "\n",
    "This section defines the file containing the project data, the number of bins that will be used in the histograms, and the range of the project data that will actually be used (in this case, some data is removed due to inconsistencies in suppressing the water signal)."
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",

    "data_file_name = \"mann.test\"\n",
    "\n",
    "#The range of the data that will actually be used\n",
    "range_to_use = list(range(959)) + list(range(1058,1860)) # This removes an extra region around the water signal region\n",
    "#range_to_use = None\n",
    "\n",
    "#Number of bins for the histogram\n",
    "num_bins = 20"
   ]

    "Distance metrics\n",
    "----------------\n",
    "\n",
    "The interspectral distance metrics used to calculate "
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 5,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": true
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "jeffries = r'Symmetric Kullback-Liebler'\n",
    "jensen = r'Jensen-Shannon'\n",
    "hellinger = r'Hellinger'\n",
    "mahalanobis = r'Mahalanobis'\n",
    "nmr_distance_metrics = [dict(metric=mahalanobis,function='mahalanobis'),\n",
    "                        dict(metric=hellinger,function=qmet.hellinger_hyp),\n",
    "                        dict(metric=jeffries,function=qmet.jeffries),\n",
    "                        dict(metric=jensen,function=qmet.jensen_hyp)\n",
    "                       ]"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "raw",

    "raw_mimetype": "text/restructuredtext"
   },

    "--------------------"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 6,
   "metadata": {
    "collapsed": true
   },

   "source": [

    "                                    Sample_names=Spectrum_names,\n",
    "                                    Data_set_names=Labels,\n",
    "                                    distance_metric_dict=nmr_distance_metrics,\n",
    "                                    range_to_use=range_to_use\n",
    "                                   )\n"
   ]
